<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a> (36263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:article.html>article</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a>:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brill_(fish)" class="extiw" title="w:brill (fish)"><a href = vnd.unilang:brill.html>brill</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:fish.html>fish</a>)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brill_(fish)" class="extiw" title="w:brill (fish)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>Possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cornish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Cornish language">Cornish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brilli</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mackerel.html>mackerel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brithelli</i>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brithel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mackerel.html>mackerel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw">brith</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spotted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:abbreviation.html>Abbreviation</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brilliant.html>brilliant</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
